  <script type="text/javascript">
   $(window).load(function () {
        /* 20190225 modify header 수정 */
        
        /**-- Gnb_opener  ---**/
        var $stickyNavOffset, $windowEl = $('#window');
        if ($windowEl.length) {
            $('.gnb_opener button').on('click', function () {
                $('body').toggleClass('window');
                var $stickyNavClear = setTimeout(function () {
                    $stickyNavOffset = $('header #top_banner').outerHeight() + $('header .global-search').outerHeight();
                    stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
                    clearTimeout($stickyNavClear);
                }, 50);
            });
        } else {
            $stickyNavOffset = $('header nav').offset().top;
            stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
        }

        /**-- Sticky nav search  --**/
        $('header nav .utility li.nav_search').on('click', function () {
            TweenMax.to('#top_search.header-fixed', .4, { className: '+=active' });
        }).find('a').on('click', function (e) {
            e.preventDefault();
        });

        /**-- Sticky navigation --**/
        function stickyNavFunc(offsetTop) {
            var $scrollTop = $(window).scrollTop();

            if ($scrollTop >= offsetTop) {
                $('header nav').addClass('fixed');
                $('#top_search').addClass('header-fixed');
                $('header nav .symbol, header nav .utility, #container').addClass('active');

                //window
                if ($windowEl.length) {
                    $('.gnb_opener').addClass('active');
                    $windowEl.addClass('active')
                        .find('.btn_list_open').addClass('active');
                }
            } else {
                $('header nav').removeClass('fixed');
                $('#top_search').removeClass('header-fixed');
                $('header nav .symbol, header nav .utility, #container').removeClass('active');

                //window
                if ($windowEl.length) {
                    $('.gnb_opener').removeClass('active');
                    $windowEl.removeClass('active')
                        .find('.btn_list_open').removeClass('active');
                }
            }
        }
        /* end // 20190225 modify header 수정 */

        /**-- Main top banner  --**/
        var main_bannerBtn = 0;
        $('#top_banner .btn-wrap').on('click', function () {
            if (main_bannerBtn === 0) {
                $(this).parents().find('.banner').removeClass('active');
                $(this).children('.icon.icon_up').removeClass('active')
                    .siblings('.icon.icon_down').addClass('active');
                main_bannerBtn = 1;
            } else {
                $(this).parents().find('.banner').addClass('active');
                $(this).children('.icon.icon_up').addClass('active')
                    .siblings('.icon.icon_down').removeClass('active');
                main_bannerBtn = 0;
            }
            return $stickyNavOffset = $('header nav').offset().top;
        });
        $(window).on("scroll", function () {
            stickyNavFunc($stickyNavOffset);
        });

        //와이즈 트래커 GNB 클릭 트래킹
        $('.second-nav li').on('click', function (e) {
            try {
                var trkCd = "";
                var $this = $(this);
                var $nav = $this.parents('li');
                var catlarge;
                var cateIdx;

                var $area;
                cateIdx = $nav.prevAll().length;
                catlarge = $nav.children('a').find('span').text().toUpperCase();
                catmid = "";
                $area = $this.parent().attr('class');
                switch (cateIdx) {
                    case 0:
                        if ($this.find('strong').text() == "JUST ARRIVED") {
                            trkCd = 'NEW^JUST ARRIVED';
                        }
                        else if ($area === undefined) {
                            trkCd = 'NEW^' + ($this.index() + 1) + '번상품';
                        }
                        break;
                    case 4:
                        if ($this.find('strong').text() == "SALE") {
                            trkCd = 'SALE^SALE';
                        }
                        break;
                    default:
                        if ($area == "depth3") {
                            if ($this.index() == 0) {
                                trkCd = catlarge + '^' + $this.find('strong').text();
                            } else {
                                catmid = $this.parent().children().first().find('strong').text();
                                trkCd = catlarge + '^' + catmid + '^' + $this.find('a').text();
                            }
                        }
                        else if ($area === undefined) {
                            trkCd = catlarge + '^' + ($this.index() + 1) + '번' + (catlarge == "BRAND" ? '브랜드' : '상품');
                        }
                        break;
                }
                if (trkCd != "") {
                    //_trk_flashEnvView('_TRK_CP=^GNB^' + trkCd);   // WiseTracker 제거
                }
            } catch (_e) { }
        });
    });

    function SearchKwd(kwd) {
        document.location.href = "/Search?kwd=" + encodeURI(kwd);
        return false;
    }
  </script>

                    // align height center
                    var $vt = $('.carousel .txt');
                    for (var i = 0; i < $vt.length; i++) {
                        var $height = $vt.eq(i);
                        var helf = $height.height() / 2;
                        $vt.eq(i).css('margin-top', '-' + helf + 'px');
                    };

                    var $slide = $('.carousel:not(.designers_slide)').ixSlideMax();
                    $(window).on('resize', function (e) {
                        $slide.ixSlideMax('resize');
                    });

                    var designerSlide = (function () {
                        var $dsnSlide = $('.designers_slide'),
                            $paging = $dsnSlide.find('.paging > li');

                        var currentIndex = 0,
                            length = $dsnSlide.find('ul > .ix-list-item').length,
                            isMove = false,
                            pagingWidth = 0,
                            guide0 = 0,
                            guide1 = 0;

                        var designersSlide = $('.designers_slide').ixSlideMax();

                        $(window).on('resize', function () {
                            designersSlide.ixSlideMax('resize');
                            guide0 = parseInt($dsnSlide.find('.ix-btn-prev').offset().left + $dsnSlide.find('.ix-btn-prev').outerWidth());
                            guide1 = parseInt($dsnSlide.find('.ix-btn-next').offset().left);
                            moveMenu(currentIndex);

                            var pagingRight = parseInt($paging.parent().offset().left) + pagingWidth - 15;
                            if (pagingRight < guide1) {
                                $paging.parent().stop().animate({
                                    marginLeft: parseInt($paging.parent().css('margin-left')) + guide1 - pagingRight
                                }, 300);
                            }
                        });

                        $dsnSlide.on('ixSlideMax:slideStart', function (e) {
                        });

                        $dsnSlide.on('ixSlideMax:change', function (e) {
                            isMove = false;
                            currentIndex = e.currentIndex;
                            activateMenu(currentIndex);
                            moveMenu(currentIndex);
                        });

                        //좌우 이정표 클릭시
                        $('.ix-btn-prev, .ix-btn-next').on('click', function (e) {
                            var curIdx = currentIndex;

                            var type = $(e.currentTarget).attr('class');
                            if (!isMove) {
                                isMove = true;
                                if (type.indexOf('prev') > -1) {
                                    curIdx--;
                                    if (curIdx < 0) {
                                        curIdx = length - 1;
                                    }
                                } else {
                                    curIdx++;
                                    if (curIdx > length - 1) {
                                        curIdx = 0
                                    }
                                }
                                setBgColor(curIdx);
                            }
                        });

                        //브랜드명 클릭 시
                        $paging.find('a').on('click', function (e) {
                            var idx = $(this).parent().index();

                            if (!isMove) {
                                isMove = true;
                                currentIndex = idx;
                                activateMenu(currentIndex);
                                $dsnSlide.ixSlideMax('changeIndex', currentIndex);
                            }
                            setBgColor(currentIndex);
                            e.preventDefault();
                        });
                        $paging.eq(currentIndex).find('a').trigger('click');
                        isMove = false;

                        function activateMenu(idx) {
                            $paging.removeClass('active');
                            $paging.eq(idx).addClass('active');
                        }

                        function moveMenu(idx) {
                            var $menu = $paging.eq(idx),
                                menuLeft = parseInt($menu.offset().left);
                            menuRight = menuLeft + parseInt($menu.width()),
                                pos = 0;

                            if (guide0 > menuLeft) {
                                pos = guide0 - menuLeft;
                            } else if (guide1 < menuRight) {
                                pos = -1 * (menuRight - guide1);
                            }

                            $paging.parent().stop().animate({
                                marginLeft: parseInt($paging.parent().css('margin-left')) + pos
                            }, 300);
                        }

                        //필요하다면 color[i] = SiteUtils.SetColorCode(WDesignbannerPageDS.Tables[0].Rows[i]["banner_bgcolor"].ToString()); 참조.
                        function setBgColor(idx) {
                            $dsnSlide.parent().css('background-color', arrDesignersBgColor[idx]);
                        }

                        /** ===== init ===== */
                        $paging.each(function () {
                            pagingWidth += $(this).width() + 15;
                        }).parent().width(pagingWidth);

                        $(window).trigger('resize');
                    })();

                    var _mod = (Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) + 1) % 4;
                    if (_mod == 0) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.bestPickClick('1');
                    } else if (_mod == 1) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.bestPickClick('2');
                    } else if (_mod == 2) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.bestPickClick('10');

                    } else if (_mod == 5) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.bestPickClick('199');
                    }

                    _mod = (Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) + 1) % 4;
                    if (_mod == 0) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.topSellerClick('001');
                    } else if (_mod == 1) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.topSellerClick('002');
                    } else if (_mod == 2) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.topSellerClick('004');
                    } else if (_mod == 3) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.topSellerClick('003');
                    } else if (_mod == 4) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.topSellerClick('005');
                    } else if (_mod == 5) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.topSellerClick('006');
                    }

                    _mod = (Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) + 1) % 4;
                    if (_mod == 0) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.whatsNewClick('1');
                    } else if (_mod == 1) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.whatsNewClick('2');
                    } else if (_mod == 2) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.whatsNewClick('10');
                    } else if (_mod == 3) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.whatsNewClick('9');
                    } else if (_mod == 4) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.whatsNewClick('198');
                    } else if (_mod == 5) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.whatsNewClick('199');
                    }

                    _mod = (Math.floor(Math.random() * 10) + 1) % 4;
                    if (_mod == 0) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.mustHaveClick('1');
                    } else if (_mod == 1) {
                        WCK_CMM_SHOP_RENEWAL_FN.mustHaveClick('2');

                });
